;;; Truth functions
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_c2w',C],[/,C,[-,1,C]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_c2w $C) 
    (/ $C 
      (- 1 $C)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_w2c',W],[/,W,[+,W,1]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_w2c $W) 
    (/ $W 
      (+ $W 1)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Deduction',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[[*,F1,F2],[*,[*,F1,F2],[*,C1,C2]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Deduction 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (* $F1 $F2) 
      (* 
        (* $F1 $F2) 
        (* $C1 $C2))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Abduction',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[F2,['Truth_w2c',[*,[*,F1,C1],C2]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Abduction 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ($F2 
      (Truth_w2c 
        (* 
          (* $F1 $C1) $C2))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Induction',T1,T2],['Truth_Abduction',T2,T1]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T2 $T1))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Exemplification',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[1.0,['Truth_w2c',[*,[*,F1,F2],[*,C1,C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Exemplification 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (1.0 
      (Truth_w2c 
        (* 
          (* $F1 $F2) 
          (* $C1 $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T],['Truth_Deduction',T,[1.0,0.9]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T 
      (1.0 0.9)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Negation',[F,C]],[[-,1,F],C]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Negation 
      ($F $C)) 
    ( (- 1 $F) $C))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth','StructuralDeductionNegated',T],['Truth_Negation',['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (Truth StructuralDeductionNegated $T) 
    (Truth_Negation 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Intersection',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[[*,F1,F2],[*,C1,C2]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Intersection 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (* $F1 $F2) 
      (* $C1 $C2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T],['Truth_Intersection',T,[1.0,0.9]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T 
      (1.0 0.9)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_or',A,B],[-,1,[*,[-,1,A],[-,1,B]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_or $A $B) 
    (- 1 
      (* 
        (- 1 $A) 
        (- 1 $B))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Comparison',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[let,F0,['Truth_or',F1,F2],[['If',[==,F0,0.0],0.0,[/,[*,F1,F2],F0]],['Truth_w2c',[*,F0,[*,C1,C2]]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Comparison 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let $F0 
      (Truth_or $F1 $F2) 
      ( (If 
          (== $F0 0.0) 0.0 
          (/ 
            (* $F1 $F2) $F0)) 
        (Truth_w2c 
          (* $F0 
            (* $C1 $C2))))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Analogy',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[[*,F1,F2],[*,[*,C1,C2],F2]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Analogy 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (* $F1 $F2) 
      (* 
        (* $C1 $C2) $F2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Resemblance',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[[*,F1,F2],[*,[*,C1,C2],['Truth_or',F1,F2]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Resemblance 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (* $F1 $F2) 
      (* 
        (* $C1 $C2) 
        (Truth_or $F1 $F2))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Union',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[['Truth_or',F1,F2],[*,C1,C2]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Union 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (Truth_or $F1 $F2) 
      (* $C1 $C2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Difference',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[[*,F1,[-,1,F2]],[*,C1,C2]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Difference 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (* $F1 
        (- 1 $F2)) 
      (* $C1 $C2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_DecomposePNN',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[let,Fn,[*,F1,[-,1,F2]],[[-,1,Fn],[*,Fn,[*,C1,C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_DecomposePNN 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let $Fn 
      (* $F1 
        (- 1 $F2)) 
      ( (- 1 $Fn) 
        (* $Fn 
          (* $C1 $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_DecomposeNPP',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[let,F,[*,[-,1,F1],F2],[F,[*,F,[*,C1,C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_DecomposeNPP 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let $F 
      (* 
        (- 1 $F1) $F2) 
      ($F 
        (* $F 
          (* $C1 $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_DecomposePNP',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[let,F,[*,F1,[-,1,F2]],[F,[*,F,[*,C1,C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_DecomposePNP 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let $F 
      (* $F1 
        (- 1 $F2)) 
      ($F 
        (* $F 
          (* $C1 $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_DecomposePPP',V1,V2],['Truth_DecomposeNPP',['Truth_Negation',V1],V2]])
  (= 
    (Truth_DecomposePPP $V1 $V2) 
    (Truth_DecomposeNPP 
      (Truth_Negation $V1) $V2))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_DecomposeNNN',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[let,Fn,[*,[-,1,F1],[-,1,F2]],[[-,1,Fn],[*,Fn,[*,C1,C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_DecomposeNNN 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let $Fn 
      (* 
        (- 1 $F1) 
        (- 1 $F2)) 
      ( (- 1 $Fn) 
        (* $Fn 
          (* $C1 $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Eternalize',[F,C]],[F,['Truth_w2c',C]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Eternalize 
      ($F $C)) 
    ($F 
      (Truth_w2c $C)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Revision',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],['let*',[[W1,['Truth_c2w',C1]],[W2,['Truth_c2w',C2]],[W,[+,W1,W2]],[F,[/,[+,[*,W1,F1],[*,W2,F2]],W]],[C,['Truth_w2c',W]]],[[min,1.0,F],[min,0.99,[max,[max,C,C1],C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Revision 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let* 
      ( ($W1 
          (Truth_c2w $C1)) 
        ($W2 
          (Truth_c2w $C2)) 
        ($W 
          (+ $W1 $W2)) 
        ($F 
          (/ 
            (+ 
              (* $W1 $F1) 
              (* $W2 $F2)) $W)) 
        ($C 
          (Truth_w2c $W))) 
      ( (min 1.0 $F) 
        (min 0.99 
          (max 
            (max $C $C1) $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Expectation',[F,C]],[+,[*,C,[-,F,0.5]],0.5]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Expectation 
      ($F $C)) 
    (+ 
      (* $C 
        (- $F 0.5)) 0.5))


;;;NAL-1
;;;!Syllogistic rules for Inheritance:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,B],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[A,-->,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A --> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($A --> $C) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,B],T1],[[A,-->,C],T2]],[[C,-->,B],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A --> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($A --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $B) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,C],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[B,-->,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A --> $C) $T1) 
      ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($B --> $A) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,B],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[C,-->,A],['Truth_Exemplification',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A --> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $A) 
      (Truth_Exemplification $T1 $T2)))


;;;NAL-2
;;;!Rules for Similarity:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,<->,P],T]],[[P,<->,S],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S <-> $P) $T)) 
    ( ($P <-> $S) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,<->,P],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[S,<->,P],['Truth_Resemblance',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M <-> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <-> $P) 
      (Truth_Resemblance $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,-->,M],T2]],[[S,<->,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <-> $P) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,S],T2]],[[S,<->,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> $S) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <-> $P) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[S,-->,P],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S --> $P) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,S],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P --> $S) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Dealing with properties and instances:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,['{...}',['$P']]],T]],[[S,<->,['{...}',['$P']]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S --> 
          { $P }) $T)) 
            ( ($S <-> 
                { $P }) 
                  (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[['[...]',['$S']]],-->,P],T]],[[[['[...]',['$S']]],<->,P],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ( [ $S ]) --> $P) $T)) 
              ( ( ( [ $S ]) <-> $P) 
                      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$M']],-->,P],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[['{...}',['$S']],-->,P],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( { $M } --> $P) $T1) 
            ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
            ( ( { $S } --> $P) 
                  (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,[['[...]',['$M']]]],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,[['[...]',['$S']]]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P --> 
          ( [ $M ])) $T1) 
              ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
              ( ($P --> 
                  ( [ $S ])) 
                      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$A']],<->,['{...}',['$B']]]],[A,<->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( { $A } <-> 
            { $B })) 
              ($A <-> $B) 
              (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[['[...]',['$A']]],<->,[['[...]',['$B']]]]],[A,<->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ( [ $A ]) <-> 
              ( [ $B ]))) 
                  ($A <-> $B) 
                  (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


;;;NAL-3
;;;!Set decomposition:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$A','$B']],-->,M],T]],[[['{...}',['$A']],-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( { $A $B } --> $M) $T)) 
            ( ( { $A } --> $M) 
                  (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$A','$B']],-->,M],T]],[[['{...}',['$B']],-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( { $A $B } --> $M) $T)) 
            ( ( { $B } --> $M) 
                  (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[['M',-->,[['[...]',['$A','$B']]]],T]],[['M',-->,[['[...]',['$A']]]],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( (M --> 
          ( [ $A $B ])) $T)) 
              ( (M --> 
                  ( [ $A ])) 
                      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[['M',-->,[['[...]',['$A','$B']]]],T]],[['M',-->,[['[...]',['$B']]]],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( (M --> 
          ( [ $A $B ])) $T)) 
              ( (M --> 
                  ( [ $B ])) 
                      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


;;;!Extensional and intensional intersection decomposition:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T]],[[S,-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($S | $P) --> $M) $T)) 
    ( ($S --> $M) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,[S,&,P]],T]],[[M,-->,S],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S & $P)) $T)) 
    ( ($M --> $S) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($S | $P) --> $M) $T)) 
    ( ($P --> $M) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,[S,&,P]],T]],[[M,-->,P],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S & $P)) $T)) 
    ( ($M --> $P) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,~,S],-->,M],T]],[[A,-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A ~ $S) --> $M) $T)) 
    ( ($A --> $M) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,[B,-,S]],T]],[[M,-->,B],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($B - $S)) $T)) 
    ( ($M --> $B) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,~,S],-->,M],T]],[[S,-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeductionNegated',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A ~ $S) --> $M) $T)) 
    ( ($S --> $M) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeductionNegated $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,[B,-,S]],T]],[[M,-->,S],['Truth_StructuralDeductionNegated',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($B - $S)) $T)) 
    ( ($M --> $S) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeductionNegated $T)))


;;;!Extensional and intensional intersection composition: (sets via reductions)
;;(= (|- (($P --> $M) $T1) (($S --> $M) $T2)) ((($P | $S) --> $M) (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- (($P --> $M) $T1) (($S --> $M) $T2)) ((($P & $S) --> $M) (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- (($P --> $M) $T1) (($S --> $M) $T2)) ((($P ~ $S) --> $M) (Truth_Difference $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- (($M --> $P) $T1) (($M --> $S) $T2)) (($M --> ($P & $S)) (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- (($M --> $P) $T1) (($M --> $S) $T2)) (($M --> ($P | $S)) (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- (($M --> $P) $T1) (($M --> $S) $T2)) (($M --> ($P - $S)) (Truth_Difference $T1 $T2)))
;;;!Extensional and intensional intersection decomposition:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,M],T1],[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($S | $P) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T2]],[[S,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($S | $P) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,M],T1],[[[S,&,P],-->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($S & $P) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[[S,&,P],-->,M],T2]],[[S,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($S & $P) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,M],T1],[[[S,~,P],-->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposePNP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($S ~ $P) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,M],T1],[[[P,~,S],-->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposeNNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($P ~ $S) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,S],T1],[[M,-->,[S,&,P]],T2]],[[M,-->,P],['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $S) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S & $P)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $P) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,[S,&,P]],T2]],[[M,-->,S],['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S & $P)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $S) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,S],T1],[[M,-->,[S,'|',P]],T2]],[[M,-->,P],['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $S) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S | $P)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $P) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,[S,'|',P]],T2]],[[M,-->,S],['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S | $P)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $S) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,S],T1],[[M,-->,[S,-,P]],T2]],[[M,-->,P],['Truth_DecomposePNP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $S) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S - $P)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $P) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,S],T1],[[M,-->,[P,-,S]],T2]],[[M,-->,P],['Truth_DecomposeNNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $S) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($P - $S)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $P) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNNN $T1 $T2)))


;;; NAL-4
;;;!Transformation rules between product and image:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T]],[[A,-->,[R,'/1',B]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T)) 
    ( ($A --> 
        ($R /1 $B)) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T]],[[B,-->,[R,'/2',A]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T)) 
    ( ($B --> 
        ($R /2 $A)) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T]],[[[R,'\\1',B],-->,A],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T)) 
    ( ( ($R \1 $B) --> $A) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T]],[[[R,'\\2',A],-->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T)) 
    ( ( ($R \2 $A) --> $B) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


;;;other direction of same rules (as these are bi-directional)

;;(= (|- ((($R \2 $A) --> $B) $T)) (($R --> ($A * $B)) (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))
;;;!Comparative relations
;;(= (|- ((({ $R }) |-> ([ $P ])) $T1) ((({ $S }) |-> ([ $P ])) $T2)) (((({ $R }) * ({ $S })) --> (>>> $P )) (Truth_FrequencyGreater $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- ((($A * $B) --> (>>> $P)) $T1) ((($B * $C) --> (>>> $P)) $T2)) ((($A * $C) --> (>>> $P)) (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- ((({ $R }) |-> ([ $P ])) $T1) ((({ $S }) |-> ([ $P ])) $T2)) (((({ $R }) * ({ $S })) --> (=== $P)) (Truth_FrequencyEqual $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- ((($A * $B) --> (=== $P)) $T1) ((($B * $C) --> (=== $P)) $T2)) ((($A * $C) --> (=== $P)) (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- ((($A * $B) --> (=== $P)) $T)) ((($B * $A) --> (=== $P)) (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))
;;;!Optional rules for more efficient reasoning about relation components:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],T2]],[[C,-->,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $A) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],T2]],[[C,-->,B],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $B) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],T2]],[[C,-->,A],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($C * $B)) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $A) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],T2]],[[C,-->,B],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $C)) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $B) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,-->,A],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($C --> $A) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[A,-->,C],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($A --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,<->,A],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($C <-> $A) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,-->,B],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($C --> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,<->,B],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($C <-> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[A,-->,C],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($A --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($C * $B)) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,-->,A],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C --> $A) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($C * $B)) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,<->,A],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C <-> $A) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($C * $B)) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $C)) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,-->,B],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C --> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $C)) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,<->,B],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C <-> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $C)) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],T2]],[[A,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) $T2)) 
    ( ($A <-> $C) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],T2]],[[B,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) $T2)) 
    ( ($B <-> $C) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],T2]],[[A,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($C * $B)) $T2)) 
    ( ($A <-> $C) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],T2]],[[B,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $C)) $T2)) 
    ( ($B <-> $C) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


;;;NAL-5
;;;!Negation conjunction and disjunction decomposition:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[!,A],T]],[A,['Truth_Negation',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( (! $A) $T)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_Negation $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,&&,B],T]],[A,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A && $B) $T)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,&&,B],T]],[B,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A && $B) $T)) 
    ($B 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,&&,B],T]],[[B,&&,A],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A && $B) $T)) 
    ( ($B && $A) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[S,&&,A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ($S && $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[S,'||',A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ($S || $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[[!,S],&&,A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposeNNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ( (! $S) && $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposeNNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[[!,S],'||',A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposePPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ( (! $S) || $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposePPP $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Syllogistic rules for Implication:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[A,==>,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($A ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[A,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,B],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> $B) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[B,==>,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($B ==> $A) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,A],['Truth_Exemplification',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> $A) 
      (Truth_Exemplification $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Conditional composition for conjunction and disjunction:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,&&,B],==>,C],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A && $B) ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,'||',B],==>,C],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A || $B) ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,&&,B]],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
      ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> 
        ($A && $B)) 
      (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,'||',B]],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
      ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> 
        ($A || $B)) 
      (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Multi-conditional inference:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[S,&&,P],==>,M],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[P,['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($S && $P) ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ($P 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,M],==>,P],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[[[C,&&,S],==>,P],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($C && $M) ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,P],==>,M],T1],[[[C,&&,S],==>,M],T2]],[[S,==>,P],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($C && $P) ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,M],==>,P],T1],[[M,==>,S],T2]],[[[C,&&,S],==>,P],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($C && $M) ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M ==> $S) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Rules for equivalence:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,<=>,P],T]],[[P,<=>,S],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S <=> $P) $T)) 
    ( ($P <=> $S) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,==>,P],T1],[[P,==>,S],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($P ==> $S) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,==>,M],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,==>,P],T1],[[M,==>,S],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M ==> $S) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,==>,P],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[S,==>,P],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,==>,M],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[P,==>,S],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P ==> $S) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,<=>,P],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Resemblance',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M <=> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Resemblance $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Higher-order decomposition
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[A,T1],[[A,==>,B],T2]],[B,['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($A $T1) 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ($B 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[A,T1],[[[A,&&,B],==>,C],T2]],[[B,==>,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($A $T1) 
      ( ( ($A && $B) ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[B,T1],[[A,==>,B],T2]],[A,['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($B $T1) 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[A,T1],[[A,<=>,B],T2]],[B,['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($A $T1) 
      ( ($A <=> $B) $T2)) 
    ($B 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


;;;NAL term reductions
;;;!Extensional intersection, union, conjunction reductions:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,&,A],A])
  (= 
    ($A & $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,'|',A],A])
  (= 
    ($A | $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,&&,A],A])
  (= 
    ($A && $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,'||',A],A])
  (= 
    ($A || $A) $A)


;;;!Extensional set reductions:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[A]],'|',['{...}',[B]]],['{...}',[A,B]]])
  (= 
    ( { $A } | 
        { $B }) 
          { $A $B })


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[A,B]],'|',['{...}',[C]]],['{...}',[[A|B],C]]])
  (= 
    ( { $A $B } | 
        { $C }) 
          { (Cons  $A $B) $C })


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[C]],'|',['{...}',[A,B]]],['{...}',[C,[A|B]]]])
  (= 
    ( { $C } | 
        { $A $B }) 
          { $C 
            (Cons  $A $B) })


;;;!Intensional set reductions:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A]]],&,[['[...]',[B]]]],[['[...]',[A,B]]]])
  (= 
    ( ( [ $A ]) & 
          ( [ $B ])) 
              ( [ $A $B ]))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A,B]]],&,[['[...]',[C]]]],[['[...]',[[A|B],C]]]])
  (= 
    ( ( [ $A $B ]) & 
          ( [ $C ])) 
              ( [ (Cons  $A $B) $C ]))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A]]],&,[['[...]',[B,C]]]],[['[...]',[A,[B|C]]]]])
  (= 
    ( ( [ $A ]) & 
          ( [ $B $C ])) 
              ( [ $A 
                  (Cons  $B $C) ]))


;;;!Reduction for set element copula:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['{...}',[[A|B]]],['{...}',[A,B]]])
  (= 
    { (Cons  $A $B) } 
      { $A $B })


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[['[...]',[[A|B]]]],[['[...]',[A,B]]]])
  (= 
    ( [ (Cons  $A $B) ]) 
        ( [ $A $B ]))

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['BoundEvents',Collection,Threshold,Increment,TargetAmount,T],[sequential,[[do,['let*',[[Ev,['get-atoms',Collection]],[['Event',Sentence,[Time,Evidence,EPrio]],Ev]],['If',[<,['EventPriorityNow',EPrio,T],Threshold],['remove-atom',Collection,Ev]]]],[let,CurrentAmount,['CollapseCardinality',['get-atoms',Collection]],['If',[>,CurrentAmount,TargetAmount],['BoundEvents',Collection,[+,Threshold,Increment],Increment,TargetAmount,T]]]]]])

        (let $CurrentAmount 
          (CollapseCardinality 
            (get-atoms $Collection)) 
          (If 
            (> $CurrentAmount $TargetAmount) 
            (BoundEvents $Collection 
              (+ $Threshold $Increment) $Increment $TargetAmount $T))))))

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['StampDisjoint',X],[not,[sequential,[[do,['change-state!','&tempstate','False']],[do,[case,['get-atoms','&tempset'],[[Y,['remove-atom','&tempset',Y]]]]],[do,[let,Z,[superpose,X],[case,[match,'&tempset',Z,Z],[[W,['change-state!','&tempstate','True']],['%void%',['add-atom','&tempset',Z]]]]]],['get-state','&tempstate']]]]])

;;revise if there is no evidential overlap, else use higher-confident candidate
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['RevisionAndChoice',['Event',[Term1,[F1,C1]],[eternal,Ev1,EPrio1]],['Event',[Term2,[F2,C2]],[eternal,Ev2,EPrio2]]],[let,ConclusionStamp,['TupleConcat',Ev1,Ev2],['If',['StampDisjoint',ConclusionStamp],['Event',[Term1,['Truth_Revision',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]]],[eternal,ConclusionStamp,[0,0.0]]],['If',[>,C1,C2],['Event',[Term1,[F1,C1]],[eternal,Ev1,[0,0.0]]],['Event',[Term2,[F2,C2]],[eternal,Ev2,[0,0.0]]]]]]])
  (= 
    (RevisionAndChoice 
      (Event 
        ($Term1 
          ($F1 $C1)) 
        (eternal $Ev1 $EPrio1)) 
      (Event 
        ($Term2 
          ($F2 $C2)) 
        (eternal $Ev2 $EPrio2))) 
    (let $ConclusionStamp 
      (TupleConcat $Ev1 $Ev2) 
      (If 
        (StampDisjoint $ConclusionStamp) 
        (Event 
          ($Term1 
            (Truth_Revision 
              ($F1 $C1) 
              ($F2 $C2))) 
          (eternal $ConclusionStamp 
            (0 0.0))) 
        (If 
          (> $C1 $C2) 
          (Event 
            ($Term1 
              ($F1 $C1)) 
            (eternal $Ev1 
              (0 0.0))) 
          (Event 
            ($Term2 
              ($F2 $C2)) 
            (eternal $Ev2 
              (0 0.0)))))))


;;update beliefs in existing concept with the new event or create new concept to enter the new evidence
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['UpdateConcept',NewEvent,T],['let*',[[['Event',[Term,TV],[Time,Evidence,EPrio]],NewEvent],[NewEventEternalized,['Eternalize',NewEvent]],[MatchConcept,['Concept',Term,Belief,BeliefEvent,CPrio]]],[sequential,[[case,[match,'&attentional_focus',MatchConcept,MatchConcept],[[MatchConcept,[sequential,[['remove-atom','&attentional_focus',MatchConcept],['let*',[[['Event',RevSentence,Metadata],['RevisionAndChoice',Belief,NewEventEternalized]],[RevisedBelief,['Event',['trace!',[@,RevSentence],RevSentence],Metadata]],[MaxPrio,['If',[>,['EventPriorityNow',EPrio,T],['ConceptPriorityNow',CPrio,T]],EPrio,CPrio]]],['add-atom','&attentional_focus',['Concept',Term,RevisedBelief,NewEvent,MaxPrio]]]]]],['%void%',[case,[match,'&concepts',MatchConcept,MatchConcept],[[MatchConcept,[sequential,[['remove-atom','&concepts',MatchConcept],['add-atom','&attentional_focus',MatchConcept],['UpdateConcept',NewEvent,T]]]],['%void%',['add-atom','&attentional_focus',['Concept',Term,NewEventEternalized,NewEvent,EPrio]]]]]]]]]]]])
  (= 
    (UpdateConcept $NewEvent $T) 
    (let* 
      ( ( (Event 
            ($Term $TV) 
            ($Time $Evidence $EPrio)) $NewEvent) 
        ($NewEventEternalized 
          (Eternalize $NewEvent)) 
        ($MatchConcept 
          (Concept $Term $Belief $BeliefEvent $CPrio))) 
      (sequential 
        ( (case 
            (match &attentional_focus $MatchConcept $MatchConcept) 
            ( ($MatchConcept 
                (sequential 
                  ( (remove-atom &attentional_focus $MatchConcept) 
                    (let* 
                      ( ( (Event $RevSentence $Metadata) 
                          (RevisionAndChoice $Belief $NewEventEternalized)) 
                        ($RevisedBelief 
                          (Event 
                            (trace! 
                              (@ $RevSentence) $RevSentence) $Metadata)) 
                        ($MaxPrio 
                          (If 
                            (> 
                              (EventPriorityNow $EPrio $T) 
                              (ConceptPriorityNow $CPrio $T)) $EPrio $CPrio))) 
                      (add-atom &attentional_focus 
                        (Concept $Term $RevisedBelief $NewEvent $MaxPrio)))))) 
              (%void% 
                (case 
                  (match &concepts $MatchConcept $MatchConcept) 
                  ( ($MatchConcept 
                      (sequential 
                        ( (remove-atom &concepts $MatchConcept) 
                          (add-atom &attentional_focus $MatchConcept)

;;; stdlib extension
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'If',[->,'Bool','Atom','Atom']])
  (: If 
    (-> Bool Atom Atom))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['If','True',Then],Then])
  (= 
    (If True $Then) $Then)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['If','False',Then],[nop]])
  (= 
    (If False $Then) 
    (nop))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'If',[->,'Bool','Atom','Atom','Atom']])
  (: If 
    (-> Bool Atom Atom Atom))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['If',Cond,Then,Else],[if,Cond,Then,Else]])
  (= 
    (If $Cond $Then $Else) 
    (if $Cond $Then $Else))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['TupleConcat',Ev1,Ev2],[collapse,[superpose,[[superpose,Ev1],[superpose,Ev2]]]]])
  (= 
    (TupleConcat $Ev1 $Ev2) 
    (collapse 
      (superpose 
        ( (superpose $Ev1) 
          (superpose $Ev2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[max,Num1,Num2],['If',[>,Num1,Num2],Num1,Num2]])
  (= 
    (max $Num1 $Num2) 
    (If 
      (> $Num1 $Num2) $Num1 $Num2))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[min,Num1,Num2],['If',[<,Num1,Num2],Num1,Num2]])
  (= 
    (min $Num1 $Num2) 
    (If 
      (< $Num1 $Num2) $Num1 $Num2))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[abs,X],['If',[<,X,0],[-,0,X],X]])
  (= 
    (abs $X) 
    (If 
      (< $X 0) 
      (- 0 $X) $X))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,sequential,[->,'Expression','%Undefined%']])
  (: sequential 
    (-> Expression %Undefined%))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[sequential,Num1],[superpose,Num1]])
  (= 
    (sequential $Num1) 
    (superpose $Num1))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,do,[->,'Expression','%Undefined%']])
  (: do 
    (-> Expression %Undefined%))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[do,Num1],[case,Num1,[]]])
  (= 
    (do $Num1) 
    (case $Num1 ()))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['TupleCount',[]],0])
  (= 
    (TupleCount ()) 0)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['TupleCount',[1]],1])
  (= 
    (TupleCount 
      (1)) 1)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['BuildTupleCounts',TOld,C,N],[let,T,[collapse,[superpose,[1,[superpose,TOld]]]],[superpose,[['trace!',[=,['TupleCount',T],[+,C,2]],[]],['If',[<,C,N],['BuildTupleCounts',T,[+,C,1],N]]]]]])
  (= 
    (BuildTupleCounts $TOld $C $N) 
    (let $T 
      (collapse 
        (superpose 
          (1 
            (superpose $TOld)))) 
      (superpose 
        ( (trace! 
            (= 
              (TupleCount $T) 
              (+ $C 2)) ()) 
          (If 
            (< $C $N) 
            (BuildTupleCounts $T 
              (+ $C 1) $N))))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'CountElement',[->,'Expression','Number']])
  (: CountElement 
    (-> Expression Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['CountElement',X],[case,X,[[Y,1]]]])

    (CountElement $X) 
    (case $X 
      ( ($Y 1))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'CollapseCardinality',[->,'Expression','Number']])

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['CollapseCardinality',Expression],['TupleCount',[collapse,['CountElement',Expression]]]])

        (CountElement $Expression))))

  (= 
    (Truth_c2w $C) 
    (/ $C 
      (- 1 $C)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_w2c',W],[/,W,[+,W,1]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_w2c $W) 
    (/ $W 
      (+ $W 1)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Deduction',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[[*,F1,F2],[*,[*,F1,F2],[*,C1,C2]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Deduction 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (* $F1 $F2) 
      (* 
        (* $F1 $F2) 
        (* $C1 $C2))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Abduction',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[F2,['Truth_w2c',[*,[*,F1,C1],C2]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Abduction 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ($F2 
      (Truth_w2c 
        (* 
          (* $F1 $C1) $C2))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Induction',T1,T2],['Truth_Abduction',T2,T1]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T2 $T1))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Exemplification',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[1.0,['Truth_w2c',[*,[*,F1,F2],[*,C1,C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Exemplification 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (1.0 
      (Truth_w2c 
        (* 
          (* $F1 $F2) 
          (* $C1 $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T],['Truth_Deduction',T,[1.0,0.9]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T 
      (1.0 0.9)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Negation',[F,C]],[[-,1,F],C]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Negation 
      ($F $C)) 
    ( (- 1 $F) $C))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth','StructuralDeductionNegated',T],['Truth_Negation',['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (Truth StructuralDeductionNegated $T) 
    (Truth_Negation 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Intersection',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[[*,F1,F2],[*,C1,C2]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Intersection 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (* $F1 $F2) 
      (* $C1 $C2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T],['Truth_Intersection',T,[1.0,0.9]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T 
      (1.0 0.9)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_or',A,B],[-,1,[*,[-,1,A],[-,1,B]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_or $A $B) 
    (- 1 
      (* 
        (- 1 $A) 
        (- 1 $B))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Comparison',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[let,F0,['Truth_or',F1,F2],[['If',[==,F0,0.0],0.0,[/,[*,F1,F2],F0]],['Truth_w2c',[*,F0,[*,C1,C2]]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Comparison 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let $F0 
      (Truth_or $F1 $F2) 
      ( (If 
          (== $F0 0.0) 0.0 
          (/ 
            (* $F1 $F2) $F0)) 
        (Truth_w2c 
          (* $F0 
            (* $C1 $C2))))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Analogy',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[[*,F1,F2],[*,[*,C1,C2],F2]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Analogy 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (* $F1 $F2) 
      (* 
        (* $C1 $C2) $F2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Resemblance',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[[*,F1,F2],[*,[*,C1,C2],['Truth_or',F1,F2]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Resemblance 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (* $F1 $F2) 
      (* 
        (* $C1 $C2) 
        (Truth_or $F1 $F2))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Union',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[['Truth_or',F1,F2],[*,C1,C2]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Union 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (Truth_or $F1 $F2) 
      (* $C1 $C2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Difference',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[[*,F1,[-,1,F2]],[*,C1,C2]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Difference 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    ( (* $F1 
        (- 1 $F2)) 
      (* $C1 $C2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_DecomposePNN',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[let,Fn,[*,F1,[-,1,F2]],[[-,1,Fn],[*,Fn,[*,C1,C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_DecomposePNN 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let $Fn 
      (* $F1 
        (- 1 $F2)) 
      ( (- 1 $Fn) 
        (* $Fn 
          (* $C1 $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_DecomposeNPP',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[let,F,[*,[-,1,F1],F2],[F,[*,F,[*,C1,C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_DecomposeNPP 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let $F 
      (* 
        (- 1 $F1) $F2) 
      ($F 
        (* $F 
          (* $C1 $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_DecomposePNP',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[let,F,[*,F1,[-,1,F2]],[F,[*,F,[*,C1,C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_DecomposePNP 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let $F 
      (* $F1 
        (- 1 $F2)) 
      ($F 
        (* $F 
          (* $C1 $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_DecomposePPP',V1,V2],['Truth_DecomposeNPP',['Truth_Negation',V1],V2]])
  (= 
    (Truth_DecomposePPP $V1 $V2) 
    (Truth_DecomposeNPP 
      (Truth_Negation $V1) $V2))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_DecomposeNNN',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],[let,Fn,[*,[-,1,F1],[-,1,F2]],[[-,1,Fn],[*,Fn,[*,C1,C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_DecomposeNNN 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let $Fn 
      (* 
        (- 1 $F1) 
        (- 1 $F2)) 
      ( (- 1 $Fn) 
        (* $Fn 
          (* $C1 $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Eternalize',[F,C]],[F,['Truth_w2c',C]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Eternalize 
      ($F $C)) 
    ($F 
      (Truth_w2c $C)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Revision',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]],['let*',[[W1,['Truth_c2w',C1]],[W2,['Truth_c2w',C2]],[W,[+,W1,W2]],[F,[/,[+,[*,W1,F1],[*,W2,F2]],W]],[C,['Truth_w2c',W]]],[[min,1.0,F],[min,0.99,[max,[max,C,C1],C2]]]]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Revision 
      ($F1 $C1) 
      ($F2 $C2)) 
    (let* 
      ( ($W1 
          (Truth_c2w $C1)) 
        ($W2 
          (Truth_c2w $C2)) 
        ($W 
          (+ $W1 $W2)) 
        ($F 
          (/ 
            (+ 
              (* $W1 $F1) 
              (* $W2 $F2)) $W)) 
        ($C 
          (Truth_w2c $W))) 
      ( (min 1.0 $F) 
        (min 0.99 
          (max 
            (max $C $C1) $C2)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Truth_Expectation',[F,C]],[+,[*,C,[-,F,0.5]],0.5]])
  (= 
    (Truth_Expectation 
      ($F $C)) 
    (+ 
      (* $C 
        (- $F 0.5)) 0.5))


;;;NAL-1
;;;!Syllogistic rules for Inheritance:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,B],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[A,-->,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A --> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($A --> $C) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,B],T1],[[A,-->,C],T2]],[[C,-->,B],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A --> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($A --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $B) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,C],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[B,-->,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A --> $C) $T1) 
      ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($B --> $A) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,B],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[C,-->,A],['Truth_Exemplification',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A --> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $A) 
      (Truth_Exemplification $T1 $T2)))


;;;NAL-2
;;;!Rules for Similarity:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,<->,P],T]],[[P,<->,S],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S <-> $P) $T)) 
    ( ($P <-> $S) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,<->,P],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[S,<->,P],['Truth_Resemblance',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M <-> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <-> $P) 
      (Truth_Resemblance $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,-->,M],T2]],[[S,<->,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <-> $P) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,S],T2]],[[S,<->,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> $S) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <-> $P) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[S,-->,P],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S --> $P) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,S],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P --> $S) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Dealing with properties and instances:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,['{...}',['$P']]],T]],[[S,<->,['{...}',['$P']]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S --> 
          { $P }) $T)) 
            ( ($S <-> 
                { $P }) 
                  (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[['[...]',['$S']]],-->,P],T]],[[[['[...]',['$S']]],<->,P],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ( [ $S ]) --> $P) $T)) 
              ( ( ( [ $S ]) <-> $P) 
                      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$M']],-->,P],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[['{...}',['$S']],-->,P],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( { $M } --> $P) $T1) 
            ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
            ( ( { $S } --> $P) 
                  (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,[['[...]',['$M']]]],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,[['[...]',['$S']]]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P --> 
          ( [ $M ])) $T1) 
              ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
              ( ($P --> 
                  ( [ $S ])) 
                      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$A']],<->,['{...}',['$B']]]],[A,<->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( { $A } <-> 
            { $B })) 
              ($A <-> $B) 
              (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[['[...]',['$A']]],<->,[['[...]',['$B']]]]],[A,<->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ( [ $A ]) <-> 
              ( [ $B ]))) 
                  ($A <-> $B) 
                  (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))

;;;!Set decomposition:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$A','$B']],-->,M],T]],[[['{...}',['$A']],-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (=

;;;!Extensional and intensional intersection decomposition:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T]],[[S,-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])

    ( ($S --> $M)

  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S & $P)) $T)) 
    ( ($M --> $S) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])

      ( ( ($S | $P) --> $M) $T)) 
    ( ($P --> $M)

    (|- 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S & $P)) $T)) 
    ( ($M --> $P) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,~,S],-->,M],T]],[[A,-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A ~ $S) --> $M) $T)) 
    ( ($A --> $M) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,[B,-,S]],T]],[[M,-->,B],['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($B - $S)) $T)) 
    ( ($M --> $B)

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,~,S],-->,M],T]],[[S,-->,M],['Truth_StructuralDeductionNegated',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A ~ $S) --> $M) $T)) 
    ( ($S --> $M) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeductionNegated $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,[B,-,S]],T]],[[M,-->,S],['Truth_StructuralDeductionNegated',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($B - $S)) $T)) 
    ( ($M --> $S) 
      (Truth_StructuralDeductionNegated $T)))


;;;!Extensional and intensional intersection composition: (sets via reductions)
;;(= (|- (($P --> $M) $T1) (($S --> $M) $T2)) ((($P | $S) --> $M) (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- (($P --> $M) $T1) (($S --> $M) $T2)) ((($P & $S) --> $M) (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- (($P --> $M) $T1) (($S --> $M) $T2)) ((($P ~ $S) --> $M) (Truth_Difference $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- (($M --> $P) $T1) (($M --> $S) $T2)) (($M --> ($P & $S)) (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- (($M --> $P) $T1) (($M --> $S) $T2)) (($M --> ($P | $S)) (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- (($M --> $P) $T1) (($M --> $S) $T2)) (($M --> ($P - $S)) (Truth_Difference $T1 $T2)))
;;;!Extensional and intensional intersection decomposition:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,M],T1],[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($S | $P) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T2]],[[S,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($S | $P) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,M],T1],[[[S,&,P],-->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($S & $P) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[[S,&,P],-->,M],T2]],[[S,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($S & $P) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,M],T1],[[[S,~,P],-->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposePNP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($S ~ $P) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,M],T1],[[[P,~,S],-->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposeNNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S --> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($P ~ $S) --> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P --> $M) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,S],T1],[[M,-->,[S,&,P]],T2]],[[M,-->,P],['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $S) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S & $P)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $P) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,[S,&,P]],T2]],[[M,-->,S],['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S & $P)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $S) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,S],T1],[[M,-->,[S,'|',P]],T2]],[[M,-->,P],['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $S) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S | $P)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $P) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,[S,'|',P]],T2]],[[M,-->,S],['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S | $P)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $S) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,S],T1],[[M,-->,[S,-,P]],T2]],[[M,-->,P],['Truth_DecomposePNP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $S) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($S - $P)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $P) 
      (Truth_DecomposePNP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,S],T1],[[M,-->,[P,-,S]],T2]],[[M,-->,P],['Truth_DecomposeNNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M --> $S) $T1) 
      ( ($M --> 
          ($P - $S)) $T2)) 
    ( ($M --> $P) 
      (Truth_DecomposeNNN $T1 $T2)))


;;; NAL-4
;;;!Transformation rules between product and image:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T]],[[A,-->,[R,'/1',B]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T)) 
    ( ($A --> 
        ($R /1 $B)) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T]],[[B,-->,[R,'/2',A]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T)) 
    ( ($B --> 
        ($R /2 $A)) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T]],[[[R,'\\1',B],-->,A],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T)) 
    ( ( ($R \1 $B) --> $A) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T]],[[[R,'\\2',A],-->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T)) 
    ( ( ($R \2 $A) --> $B) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


;;;other direction of same rules (as these are bi-directional)
;;(= (|- (($A --> ($R /1 $B)) $T)) ((($A * $B) --> $R) (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))
;;(= (|- (($B --> ($R /2 $A)) $T)) ((($A * $B) --> $R) (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))
;;(= (|- ((($R \1 $B) --> $A) $T)) (($R --> ($A * $B)) (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))
;;(= (|- ((($R \2 $A) --> $B) $T)) (($R --> ($A * $B)) (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))
;;;!Comparative relations
;;(= (|- ((({ $R }) |-> ([ $P ])) $T1) ((({ $S }) |-> ([ $P ])) $T2)) (((({ $R }) * ({ $S })) --> (>>> $P )) (Truth_FrequencyGreater $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- ((($A * $B) --> (>>> $P)) $T1) ((($B * $C) --> (>>> $P)) $T2)) ((($A * $C) --> (>>> $P)) (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- ((({ $R }) |-> ([ $P ])) $T1) ((({ $S }) |-> ([ $P ])) $T2)) (((({ $R }) * ({ $S })) --> (=== $P)) (Truth_FrequencyEqual $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- ((($A * $B) --> (=== $P)) $T1) ((($B * $C) --> (=== $P)) $T2)) ((($A * $C) --> (=== $P)) (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))
;;(= (|- ((($A * $B) --> (=== $P)) $T)) ((($B * $A) --> (=== $P)) (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))
;;;!Optional rules for more efficient reasoning about relation components:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],T2]],[[C,-->,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $A) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],T2]],[[C,-->,B],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $B) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],T2]],[[C,-->,A],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($C * $B)) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $A) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],T2]],[[C,-->,B],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $C)) $T2)) 
    ( ($C --> $B) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,-->,A],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($C --> $A) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[A,-->,C],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($A --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,<->,A],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($C <-> $A) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,-->,B],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($C --> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,<->,B],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ($C <-> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[A,-->,C],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($A --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($C * $B)) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,-->,A],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C --> $A) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($C * $B)) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,<->,A],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C <-> $A) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($C * $B)) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $C)) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,-->,B],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C --> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $C)) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,<->,B],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C <-> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $C)) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],T2]],[[A,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) $T2)) 
    ( ($A <-> $C) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],T2]],[[B,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) $T2)) 
    ( ($B <-> $C) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],T2]],[[A,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($C * $B)) $T2)) 
    ( ($A <-> $C) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],T2]],[[B,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $C)) $T2)) 
    ( ($B <-> $C) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


;;;NAL-5
;;;!Negation conjunction and disjunction decomposition:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[!,A],T]],[A,['Truth_Negation',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( (! $A) $T)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_Negation $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,&&,B],T]],[A,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A && $B) $T)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,&&,B],T]],[B,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A && $B) $T)) 
    ($B 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,&&,B],T]],[[B,&&,A],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A && $B) $T)) 
    ( ($B && $A) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[S,&&,A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ($S && $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[S,'||',A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ($S || $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[[!,S],&&,A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposeNNN',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ( (! $S) && $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposeNNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[S,T1],[[[!,S],'||',A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposePPP',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ( (! $S) || $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposePPP $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Syllogistic rules for Implication:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[A,==>,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($A ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[A,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,B],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> $B) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[B,==>,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($B ==> $A) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,A],['Truth_Exemplification',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> $A) 
      (Truth_Exemplification $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Conditional composition for conjunction and disjunction:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,&&,B],==>,C],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A && $B) ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,'||',B],==>,C],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A || $B) ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,&&,B]],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
      ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> 
        ($A && $B)) 
      (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,'||',B]],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
      ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> 
        ($A || $B)) 
      (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Multi-conditional inference:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[S,&&,P],==>,M],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[P,['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($S && $P) ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ($P 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,M],==>,P],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[[[C,&&,S],==>,P],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($C && $M) ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,P],==>,M],T1],[[[C,&&,S],==>,M],T2]],[[S,==>,P],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($C && $P) ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[C,&&,M],==>,P],T1],[[M,==>,S],T2]],[[[C,&&,S],==>,P],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ( ($C && $M) ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M ==> $S) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Rules for equivalence:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,<=>,P],T]],[[P,<=>,S],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S <=> $P) $T)) 
    ( ($P <=> $S) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,==>,P],T1],[[P,==>,S],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($S ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($P ==> $S) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,==>,M],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,==>,P],T1],[[M,==>,S],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M ==> $S) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,==>,P],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[S,==>,P],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,==>,M],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[P,==>,S],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($P ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P ==> $S) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,<=>,P],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Resemblance',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ( ($M <=> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Resemblance $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Higher-order decomposition
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[A,T1],[[A,==>,B],T2]],[B,['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($A $T1) 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ($B 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[A,T1],[[[A,&&,B],==>,C],T2]],[[B,==>,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($A $T1) 
      ( ( ($A && $B) ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[B,T1],[[A,==>,B],T2]],[A,['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($B $T1) 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[A,T1],[[A,<=>,B],T2]],[B,['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
  (= 
    (|- 
      ($A $T1) 
      ( ($A <=> $B) $T2)) 
    ($B 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


;;;NAL term reductions
;;;!Extensional intersection, union, conjunction reductions:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,&,A],A])
  (= 
    ($A & $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,'|',A],A])
  (= 
    ($A | $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,&&,A],A])
  (= 
    ($A && $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[A,'||',A],A])
  (= 
    ($A || $A) $A)


;;;!Extensional set reductions:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[A]],'|',['{...}',[B]]],['{...}',[A,B]]])
  (= 
    ( { $A } | 
        { $B }) 
          { $A $B })


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[A,B]],'|',['{...}',[C]]],['{...}',[[A|B],C]]])
  (= 
    ( { $A $B } | 
        { $C }) 
          { (Cons  $A $B) $C })


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[['{...}',[C]],'|',['{...}',[A,B]]],['{...}',[C,[A|B]]]])
  (= 
    ( { $C } | 
        { $A $B }) 
          { $C 
            (Cons  $A $B) })


;;;!Intensional set reductions:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A]]],&,[['[...]',[B]]]],[['[...]',[A,B]]]])
  (= 
    ( ( [ $A ]) & 
          ( [ $B ])) 
              ( [ $A $B ]))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A,B]]],&,[['[...]',[C]]]],[['[...]',[[A|B],C]]]])
  (= 
    ( ( [ $A $B ]) & 
          ( [ $C ])) 
              ( [ (Cons  $A $B) $C ]))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A]]],&,[['[...]',[B,C]]]],[['[...]',[A,[B|C]]]]])
  (= 
    ( ( [ $A ]) & 
          ( [ $B $C ])) 
              ( [ $A 
                  (Cons  $B $C) ]))


;;;!Reduction for set element copula:
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['{...}',[[A|B]]],['{...}',[A,B]]])
  (= 
    { (Cons  $A $B) } 
      { $A $B })


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[['[...]',[[A|B]]]],[['[...]',[A,B]]]])
  (= 
    ( [ (Cons  $A $B) ]) 
        ( [ $A $B ]))

;;making declarative inferences on two events (task from PQ and belief from concept)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Conclude',['Event',S1,[Time1,Ev1,Prio1]],['Event',S2,[Time2,Ev2,Prio2]],CPrio,T],[let,ConclusionStamp,['TupleConcat',Ev1,Ev2],['If',['StampDisjoint',ConclusionStamp],[let,[ConcTerm,ConcTV],[superpose,[['|-',S1,S2],['|-',S2,S1]]],['Event',[ConcTerm,ConcTV],[Time1,ConclusionStamp,[T,['ConclusionPriority',['EventPriorityNow',Prio1,T],['ConceptPriorityNow',CPrio,T],ConcTV]]]]]]]])

;;find a belief for the task to generate conclusions with
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['ReasonWithTask',['Event',S1,[Time1,Ev1,Prio1]],T],[let,[Belief,CPrio],[case,['get-atoms','&attentional_focus'],[[['Concept',Term,['Event',SE2,[TimeE2,EvE2,PrioE2]],['Event',S2,[Time2,Ev2,Prio2]],CPrio],['If',[and,[not,[==,Time1,eternal]],[>,[abs,[-,Time1,Time2]],20]],[['Event',SE2,[TimeE2,EvE2,PrioE2]],Cprio],[['Event',S2,[Time2,Ev2,Prio2]],CPrio]]]]],[case,['Conclude',['Event',S1,[Time1,Ev1,Prio1]],['TemporallyAlignedBelief',Time1,Belief],CPrio,T],[[['Event',Num1,Num2],['ProcessBeliefEvent',['Event',['trace!',['.',Num1],Num1],Num2],T]]]]]])
  (= 
    (ReasonWithTask 
      (Event $S1 
        ($Time1 $Ev1 $Prio1)) $T) 
    (let 
      ($Belief $CPrio) 
      (case 
        (get-atoms &attentional_focus) 
        ( ( (Concept $Term 
              (Event $SE2 
                ($TimeE2 $EvE2 $PrioE2)) 
              (Event $S2 
                ($Time2 $Ev2 $Prio2)) $CPrio) 
            (If 
              (and 
                (not 
                  (== $Time1 eternal)) 
                (> 
                  (abs 
                    (- $Time1 $Time2)) 20)) 
              ( (Event $SE2 
                  ($TimeE2 $EvE2 $PrioE2)) $Cprio) 
              ( (Event $S2 
                  ($Time2 $Ev2 $Prio2)) $CPrio))))) 
      (case 
        (Conclude 
          (Event $S1 
            ($Time1 $Ev1 $Prio1)) 
          (TemporallyAlignedBelief $Time1 $Belief) $CPrio $T) 
        ( ( (Event $Num1 $Num2) 
            (ProcessBeliefEvent 
              (Event 
                (trace! 
                  (. $Num1) $Num1) $Num2) $T))))))
